[01:47:16] would create greater efficiencies for

[01:48:55] margining allows calculation of margin

[01:49:00] portfolio rather than by individual
[01:49:02] position. And it has the effect of
[01:49:04] lowering margin requirements for
[01:49:06] trading. Lower margin requirements
